Pleasant Hill isn't one of my favorite East Bay towns but this is one of my favorite Off the Grid locations because the area is so clean, spacious and well maintained. Ahn the Go is my favorite regular truck for sweet and savory garlicky noodles with varying toppings. There is always beer and ice cream of some sort. Usually options for lobster rolls, falafel and BBQ. Free parking!</text>
